< Review>
Brought my tahoe in for a simple smog.  Absolutely awesome staff! I forget then gentleman's name precisely, and I know I put their cars around here somewhere, but the Hispanic fellow, about 5'11-ish, heavy build, great dude! Superb customer service, his associate as well, the asian gentleman (again, sorry I forget their names).

Only needed to ask me a few questions and get the info from my vehicle and had the job done pretty quick. I was their last client for the day and I was having a hell of a time trying to prioritize a couple errands (gas cap seal was ineffective so I needed to replace first otherwise the machine would throw am immediate fault and fail the test) that nearly ended with me not being able to return for the day.

But the gentleman informed me that if I could try and make it back ASAFP, he would hold the shop open for about 15 minutes late (I think because he already had everything typed into the system and only needed to get the whip on the machine and run the test (which is relatively quick and easy process for the technician) but fortunately I was able to make it back with some time to spare and not require him to stay very late.

If you check my review log, you'll see that I don't write too many review, as I'm sure too many of us miss the opportunity to let people know how our experience was (believe me, there are MANY instances where negative reviews could clearly demonstrate that some employees absolutely trash a company's reputation or at least location, costing the business..  only God knows, how much, in the long run.

This is, for as long as I reside in the greater Sacramento area, my #1 Smog Spot! Thanks guys, stellar service and representation!</Review>

<review>Daniel from Velopro was a huge help with my first new mountain bike purchase. The staff explained the differences in models I was looking at (Santa Cruz Hightower vs Megatower) over multiple visits browsing during these interesting social distancing times. After riding them multiple times in the parking lot, they sent me on my way with a demo bike for the day. This allowed me to see it in action and determine that the fit would be comfortable. < review>
Attended their special evening exhibition and reception.
What a great event!
Exhibition of Japanese Encampment during WWII was both thorough and touching. The human spirit shines through those artifacts even after more than 70 years!
Staff at HAHS continues doing great jobs!
(BTW, good time to shoot the hippest restaurant in Hayward area!)<//review>

<text>A free small intimate museum that is educational about the main people who make up Hayward, Castro Valley, Ashland and San Lorenzo.  As an added bonus, there is a separate children area for kids to pretend to work in a grocery store, hotel, dress up and fish for fishes. A really nice place to take children and learn something yourself after eating at the Cannery, a yummy breakfast/lunch eatery.  It is connected next to the museum.</text><user>112279568049511296279</user><rate>4<//rate>< Pics>

<user_id>117334890219685967862</user_id><user_name>Sharon Luther< /user_name><time>1520542050723</time><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
If you have not recently visited the Hayward historical Museum I want to encourage you to do it now, today! The displays are just remarkable. If you are new to this area it will be very informative. If like me you have been here all your life, you will have the opportunity to enjoy historical memorabilia that is just beyond delightful. And when you visit the museum, be sure to have cited breakfast or lunch at The Cannery Cafe. Their offerings are delicious and a nutritious. Don't wait go soon!<//Review>

<Resp>None</Resp><gmap_id>0x808f93d8ee4aa475:0x33caebab23e0d369</gmap_id>< Review>
What a cute little way to spend your time during the day on a weekend. We just happened to stumble in after eating breakfast in the attached Cafe.

The museum is free for at least the next two years! It was sweet to see all the old school utensils and tools that were used in the mid-1900s. Also, it was really cool to see how a cannery works, even though it was the children's exhibit.

We stayed for a free presentation about African American civil liberties, then and now. We ended up winning a calendar in a raffle, and staying for 4 hours! It was a delightfully surprising day.<//Review>

<Name>Rebecca Chapin</Name>< Review>
Visited Hatch's lab rat room about six months ago and I catch myself comparing every room I've been to since to it. Of all the 15 or so LA escape rooms I've been to, including the ever famous 'basement', the lab rat room has hands down been the best.

The set design and room concept are both very strong. It features a lot of puzzle varieties that are rarely utilized in escape rooms so it feels fresh even to an escape room enthusiast. The amount of puzzles are also very well calculated, you won't walk away feeling like it was too easy. Definitely would recommend. The only downside is it can get pretty hot in the room, even with the portable AC units that are present.</Review>

<name>Sarah Walker< /name>< Review>
Nice park, sometimes too busy, but always worth a stop! Bathrooms are cleaned regularly, and for the most part, the trash is taken care of . The play ground is newer, the swings always work, and they even have a  basketball area plus ample parking spaces! ball field and large, fully fenced, dog run adjoins this family fun area, and its thick, dark grass is well maintained as well. This park borders a nearly year round Creek, but the safety of the children,( and their families that come here) is assured by chain link fencing.
Will definitely return!!<//Review>
